# D.0 Claims Inventory — Documentation Truth Campaign

**Sub-Phase D.0 deliverable** — read-only forensic sweep of prose artifacts. Governing document: [`CLAIMS_ARCHAEOLOGY_FRAMEWORK.md`](CLAIMS_ARCHAEOLOGY_FRAMEWORK.md). This inventory **records** false, stale, and unverifiable claims; it corrects nothing. All corrections are deferred to D.1.

| | |
|---|---|
| **Sweep date** | 2026-06-12 → 2026-06-13 |
| **HEAD at sweep** | `9693649d8` (Fluids-Integration.F.1.4 FINAL) |
| **Method** | 2-pass: poison-list grep + per-class read sweep, fanned out across 25 corpus groups (2 batches) + 2 ground-truth verifiers (workspace counts + capability/dormancy at HEAD) |
| **Claims inventoried** | 1264 load-bearing present-tense claims across 129 corpus files |
| **Source modifications** | none (this report is the only file written) |

## 1. Preamble

### 1.1 Pre-flight archaeology (verbatim)

`git log --oneline -10`:
```
9693649d8 Fluids-Integration.F.1.4 (FINAL): spawn placement, ocean horizon, flatness diagnosis - chain closure
56bafd881 Fluids-Integration.F.1.3: spawn visibility root-caused, ocean defect pass
a7bb562dc Fluids-Integration.F.1.2: demo runtime defects - resize crash, dead input, never-rendered skybox/ocean, oblong impostors
3921c1437 Fluids-Integration.F.1.1: FluidRenderer hotfix - it had never constructed on any device
499220ef9 Fluids-Integration.F.1: execution report (phase deliverable)
e4c98bb7f Fluids-Integration.F.1 WI-6/WI-7: instrumentation, first baselines, hygiene, doc corrections
c3f19e31e Fluids-Integration.F.1 WI-4: solver consolidation per gate Q3
7fb4e17b0 Fluids-Integration.F.1 WI-1/2/3/5: FluidSystem correctness repair + first GPU-execution tests
e22e7bd0a Fluids-Integration.F.0: ground-truth audit report (read-only phase deliverable)
8e1505dd8 Engine-Health-Audit.2026-06-10: full health audit + workspace-wide doc reconciliation
```

`git log --oneline -5 -- README.md docs/ CLAUDE.md`:
```
9693649d8 Fluids-Integration.F.1.4 (FINAL): spawn placement, ocean horizon, flatness diagnosis - chain closure
56bafd881 Fluids-Integration.F.1.3: spawn visibility root-caused, ocean defect pass
a7bb562dc Fluids-Integration.F.1.2: demo runtime defects - resize crash, dead input, never-rendered skybox/ocean, oblong impostors
3921c1437 Fluids-Integration.F.1.1: FluidRenderer hotfix - it had never constructed on any device
499220ef9 Fluids-Integration.F.1: execution report (phase deliverable)
```

**Reading of the pre-flight.** The only commit touching the broad prose corpus since the fluids gate is the fluids campaign's own doc-correction work (F.1 WI-6/WI-7 plus the F.0/F.1 reports under `docs/campaigns/fluids-integration/`). The last *workspace-wide* doc reconciliation is `8e1505dd8` ("Engine-Health-Audit.2026-06-10"). That reconciliation reached `README.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, the master reports and the architecture traces — but **did not reach the tracked `gh-pages/` Jekyll site or the `docs/src/` mdBook source**, which is why the poison list is still substantially live there (§4). The framework file was confirmed present at `docs/campaigns/doc-truth/CLAIMS_ARCHAEOLOGY_FRAMEWORK.md` and read in full before analysis.

### 1.2 Ground truth established this sweep (at HEAD)

Two dedicated verifier agents re-derived the contested workspace counts and capability/dormancy facts at HEAD with read-only commands (`cargo metadata`, `git grep`, `wc -l`, source reads). These are the evidence anchor for every VERIFIED/STALE classification below — **no classification rests on a document asserting a document**.

| Fact | Ground truth at HEAD | Supersedes |
|---|---|---|
| Workspace members | **130** (`cargo metadata --no-deps`); 53 names start `astraweave-`; "~51 production" is a judgment bucket | 128 / 49-production / 82+ / 129 |
| Test markers (workspace) | **~39,900** `#[test]`+`#[tokio::test]` (38,803 + 1,102) | 27,000+ / 7,600+ / 166 / 800+ |
| aw_editor markers | **9,427** (≈9,425, within tolerance) | 9,397 / 3,892 / ~6,100 |
| astraweave-fluids markers | **2,560** (2,454 src + 106 tests/) | 4,907 / 2,509 / 2,404 |
| Rust LoC | **~1.16M raw / ~892K code** (tokei) | 850K+ / 860K+ / ~150K |
| astraweave-fluids LoC | **80,222 src / 83,651 crate** | 84.5K / 46,173 |
| Toolchain | **1.89.0** (rust-toolchain.toml) | 1.73+ / 1.75.0 |
| Kani proof harnesses | **~69** `kani::proof` across 5 files | 71+ |
| Fluids solvers | **FluidSystem + PcisphSystem + WaterEffectsManager** (3). `unified_solver.rs` DELETED (`c3f19e31e`); `ResearchFluidSystem` never existed as a type | "five parallel surfaces", UnifiedSolver, ResearchFluidSystem, DFSPH/IISPH, SPH/FLIP solver |
| Caustics & foam | **real** (`caustics.rs`/`foam.rs` + WGSL, owned by WaterEffectsManager) but **zero consumers outside the fluids crate** | "live production caustics and foam" |
| HNSW | still a **linear scan** (`astraweave-embeddings/src/store.rs`); `hnsw_rs` declared default-on, never imported | "live HNSW indexing" |
| SpatialHash | doc-comment still advertises it as broadphase; real broadphase is Rapier `DefaultBroadPhase` (`lib.rs:907`); only non-test caller is `profiling_demo` | "99.96% pair reduction" as a live physics benchmark |
| `auto_save_system` | still a registered **comment-only TODO stub** | "autosaves run" |
| `safe_llm_invoke` | **zero** workspace callers outside its own tests | — |
| `FallbackOrchestrator` | **NOT dormant** — real production caller in `plan_from_llm` (**CODE-FINDING**: docs claim it is unused, and show a stale 2-arg constructor) | "FallbackOrchestrator dormant" |
| Runtime LLM default | **phi3:medium** (`orchestrator.rs:488-489`); Qwen3 needs `OLLAMA_MODEL=qwen3:8b` | "Qwen3 is the live default" |
| Networking transport | **WebSocket / tokio-tungstenite**; no QUIC/Quinn anywhere; `sign16` deleted; HMAC-SHA256 surface real & enforced (W.5 holds) | "QUIC via Quinn", "XOR sign16 current" |
| ECS scheduler | **deterministic single-threaded, 8 stages** (incl. SYNC); `ParallelSchedule` removed | "7 stages", "parallel system execution" |
| Audio buses | code: 4 channels (music/ambient/voice/sfx) + master scalar; UI exposes 4 sliders (no ambient); `lib.rs:8` doc says "4-bus (master,music,SFX,voice)" — wrong composition (**CODE-FINDING**) | "5-bus mixer" |
| hello_companion | **7** AI modes (feature-gated); example header says 7 (**CODE-FINDING** on docs) | "6 modes" |
| Build health | root `Cargo.toml` ci-excludes problematic list is **EMPTY** ("All crates now work!") | "Known Build Issues" tables |
| Orphan source still on disk | `net-ecs/src/lib_temp.rs`; `astraweave-ai/src/rag/` + `src/persona/` (undeclared modules) | — |

## 2. Inventory

One row per claim. **State** ∈ VERIFIED / STALE / FABRICATED / UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP (abbrev. UNVERIF) / ASPIRATIONAL-AS-PRESENT (abbrev. ASPIR) / NEEDS-GLOBAL. **Flags**: 🟥 POISON-LIST · 🔧 CODE-FINDING · 📒 REGISTRY-CANDIDATE.

### 3.3 Patterns observed

- **The mdBook `docs/src/` API/tutorial pages are systematically fabricated.** The `28bc94f21` Copilot wiki lineage invented whole API surfaces that exist nowhere in the code: `PerceptionSnapshot`, `AIPlan`, `trait Tool`, `AiPlanner`, `ToolExecutor`, `AudioMixer`/`SpatialSource`/`ReverbZone`, `NavmeshBuilder`/`Pathfinder`/`CrowdManager`, `PostProcessStack`, `RenderContext`, a `bevy = "0.12"` dependency, a `verdentlabs` GitHub org, and `cargo build-core`/`check-all` aliases. `navigation.md` (11/11 claims fabricated) and `api/audio.md` (7/8) are pure invented-API documents.
- **Benchmark numbers are overwhelmingly UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP, not false.** 197 C1 claims, ~75% deferred to a Criterion/Miri re-run in D.1. They are not *wrong* on their face — they lack a reproduction anchor in the sweep. The headline figures (12,700 agents, 6.48M checks/sec, 2.70 ms / 370 FPS, ECS spawn ns) recur across ≥6 documents each with no single registry owner — the exact condition D.1's registry exists to fix.
- **Self-contradiction within single documents.** `arbiter.md` states LLM-poll latency as 104.7 ns, 575 ns, and 3–5 ns on three different lines; `benchmarks.md` gives 114 ns and 43.8–52.0 ns for the same character-move metric; nav "long" path is reported faster than "medium". These are transcription drift, not measurement.
- **The fluids trace is the worst single architecture artifact** (30 bad / 45 claims). Rev 1.3 bolted a §0 correction layer on top of a body that still describes `UnifiedSolver`, `ResearchFluidSystem`, "five parallel surfaces" and DFSPH/IISPH solvers as live — the trace contradicts itself, and the body half is stale/fabricated.
- **Honest-dormancy framing largely held.** Where the active corpus (CLAUDE.md, ARCHITECTURE_MAP, the ai_pipeline/physics/persistence traces) describes HNSW-as-linear, SpatialHash-as-dormant, `auto_save_system`-as-TODO, and phi3-not-Qwen3, those statements **re-verified true at HEAD** — the trace campaign's honesty discipline worked. The poison survives mostly in surfaces that reconciliation never reached (gh-pages, docs/src, the masters roadmap, .zencoder).

Historical narration is out of scope per the framework.

## 5. D.1 handoff

### 5.1 Correction batch shape (by state)

| State | Count | D.1 action |
|---|---:|---|
| FABRICATED | 84 | Delete. Never soften to qualitative. Concentrated in `docs/src/` invented-API pages and the fluids trace body. |
| STALE | 261 | Correct in place against §1.2 ground truth; attach a `<!-- Source: CLAIMS_REGISTRY #... -->` comment. |
| ASPIRATIONAL-AS-PRESENT | 72 | Rewrite with explicit dormancy/roadmap framing (HNSW-as-linear, SpatialHash-as-dormant, caustics/foam-not-wired, Qwen3-not-default). |
| UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP | 454 | Run the per-row reproduction command (Criterion / Miri / llvm-cov / cargo-mutants), then VERIFY-or-demote. Do NOT let cost upgrade these to VERIFIED. |
| NEEDS-GLOBAL | 12 | Resolve via the §1.2 global counts; mostly map directly to STALE (128→130, 27,000→39,900). |
| VERIFIED | 381 | Leave; migrate the load-bearing numbers into the registry as the canonical owner. |

### 5.2 Files where rewrite beats patching

These are contaminated past the point of in-place correction — D.1 should regenerate them from current ground truth rather than edit row-by-row:

- **`docs/src/` mdBook API/tutorial pages** (the `28bc94f21` Copilot wiki lineage): `core-systems/navigation.md` (11/11 fabricated), `api/audio.md` (7/8), `core-systems/rendering.md` (5 fab APIs), `core-systems/physics.md`, `reference/configuration.md`, `game-dev/{first-game,save-load,scripting,companions,bosses,dialogue}.md`, `getting-started/{first-companion,requirements}.md`, `architecture/{overview,ai-native,deterministic}.md`, `dev/testing.md`. Every code sample documents an API that does not exist.
- **`gh-pages/` Jekyll site** — never reached by the 2026-06 reconciliation; carries the live `128 packages`, `27,000+ tests`, `4,907 fluids`, fabricated `A+` grade, and the fabricated `physics ── fluids` dependency edge. Regenerate `index.md`, `crates.md`, `benchmarks.md`, `architecture.md`, `physics.md`, `audio.md` from the mdBook source after the mdBook source itself is corrected (or retire the duplicate site).
- **`.zencoder/rules/repo.md`** — frozen at a Nov-2025 / v0.4.0 state (82+ crates, 166 tests, Hermes 2 Pro default, 14-panel editor, 96.9% determinism). It is an *agent-instruction* artifact (alwaysApply) — high blast radius — and wrong throughout. Rewrite from CLAUDE.md.
- **`docs/architecture/fluids.md`** — the body (post-§0) must be brought into line with §0 + the F.0/F.1 reality, or the body sections replaced. 20 STALE + 9 FABRICATED rows.

### 5.3 Registry-candidate numbers (341 flagged)

The load-bearing numbers that should become single-owner rows in `docs/claims/CLAIMS_REGISTRY.md`, after which every other document links instead of restating. Highest-recurrence headline set:

- **12,700+ agents @ 60 FPS** — recurs in ≥8 files (README, ai_pipeline, ARCHITECTURE_MAP, gh-pages, docs/src). Owner: `MASTER_BENCHMARK_REPORT.md` + hardware spec (HP Pavilion Gaming Laptop 16-a0xxx). Repro: `cargo bench -p astraweave-ai` / `-p astraweave-stress-test`.
- **~39,900 test markers / 130 members / ~51 production crates** — owner: `cargo metadata` + the test-marker count command. Resolves 128/49/27,000 poison everywhere.
- **6.48M validation checks/sec**, **2.70 ms / 370 FPS @ 1,000 entities**, **ECS spawn/iteration ns**, **59.3% weighted coverage / 14 crates ≥85%**, **977 Miri tests**, **~69 Kani proofs**, **fluids 2,560 tests / 80,222 LoC**.
- The full 341 registry-candidate rows are flagged 📒 in §2; D.1 should dedupe them by canonical value before migration.

The remaining 264 CODE-FINDING-flagged rows in §2 are instances/duplicates of the nine findings above (e.g. every `gh-pages` and `docs/src` restatement of the SpatialHash-broadphase or 4-bus-audio claim carries the flag). They resolve when the nine root findings are addressed.

## 6. Honest limits

Named gaps. A truthfully partial sweep that names its remainder is the methodology; the silent-complete sweep is the failure mode this campaign exists to eliminate.

1. **Two live-poison render-plan docs were not in any sweep group.** `docs/current/RENDERER_DEEP_ANALYSIS_AND_MEGALIGHTS_PLAN.md` and `docs/current/RENDERER_MASTER_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` carry the live `103k entities @ 60 FPS` + `10.4× Unity / 2.1-5.2× Unreal` comparatives (located via Pass-1 grep, recorded in §4) but were not read end-to-end for a full claim inventory. D.1 must sweep both.
2. **Per-crate `README.md` files were out of scope** but hold live poison: `astraweave-physics/README.md` (SpatialHash 99.96% broadphase), `astraweave-ai/README.md` (12,700+ agents), and likely others. Only the root `README.md` and `docs/README.md` were swept.
3. **`docs/audits/` is only partially covered.** The marketing group globbed `docs/_audit/` (singular) and `docs/guides/`, not `docs/audits/` (plural). `EXTERNAL_RESEARCH_COMPETITIVE_ANALYSIS.md`, `COMPREHENSIVE_AUDIT_REPORT.md`, and `EXTERNAL_RESEARCH_INDEX.md` (the competitor-comparison originals) were reached only by Pass-1 grep, not full read. Most `docs/audits/` content is historical audit narration (out of scope), but the EXTERNAL_RESEARCH pair carries present-tense comparatives.
4. **`docs/journey/**` and `docs/archive/**` were deliberately skipped** as historical narration per the framework. They hold the *bulk* of poison survivors (610k entities, 50× caching, 27,000x, the original competitor estimates). This is by design — they are not present-tense capability/status claims — but if the campaign later decides archived docs feed agent context, they are a known reservoir.
5. **All C1 performance numbers and coverage/Miri/Kani counts are UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP by policy.** D.0 does not run benchmarks, the full test suite, `cargo llvm-cov`, or Miri. Each such row carries its exact D.1 reproduction command. The risk this manages: cost must not silently upgrade a claim to VERIFIED.
6. **Test-marker counts are annotation counts, not run counts.** `#[test]`/`#[tokio::test]` line counts (including the §1.2 ground truth ~39,900) count source-text attributes, which include feature-gated and example/tool tests that may not all compile-and-run in one configuration. A true count needs `cargo test --workspace` (D.1, expensive).
7. **`docs/src/performance/benchmarks.md.new`** is a stray orphan file (a `.new` sibling of `benchmarks.md`) carrying duplicate benchmark poison; swept under the api-perf group but flagged here as a probable accidental artifact for D.1 to delete or reconcile.
8. **Claim selection was capped at ~50 load-bearing rows per group.** Dense benchmark and feature-checklist tables were grouped to one row ("table of N rows asserting X") with the omission noted in each group's sweep notes. The 1,264 rows here are the curated load-bearing set, not every sentence in the corpus.

---

*Generated 1264-row inventory from a 25-group fan-out + 2 ground-truth verifiers. Read-only: `git status` is clean except this report. Next: D.1 correction batch + `docs/claims/CLAIMS_REGISTRY.md` migration, gated on owner review of this inventory.*
